# Table


```r
mtcars %>% 
  rownames_to_column(var = "name") %>%
  gt(rowname_col = "name",  groupname_col = "cyl") %>% 
  summary_rows(columns = mpg:carb, fns = list(mean = ~ sum(.)))
```
